msg:The hotel is in a prime location, close to Jinxiang Lake Park, overlooking the lake, quiet and peaceful. It is very convenient to go to the ancient town scenic area and Wuyue Plaza for shopping and dining. This morning, I roamed the park from the back door of the hotel in the drizzle and enjoyed the natural beauty of Jiangnan. The interior decoration and hardware lighting of the room are harmoniously designed, with a five-star high-end temperament.
The service must be praised, the check-in is efficient and done in seconds, and the front desk lady Lisa took the initiative to send me a guide, which facilitated the food, accommodation and transportation in Nanxun. Thank you! When checking out, the lobby manager "Traveler" enthusiastically gave me a souvenir handbag with bottled water and sleeping spray, which was unexpectedly touching.
It is particularly worth mentioning that the original room rate only included 2 breakfasts. I brought two children and was going to consult the front desk to buy two more. Unexpectedly, the front desk lady Z directly gave us two breakfasts, which was directly touched.
All of this shows that this is a hotel that cares about the guest experience. The thoughtful attention to details makes people not only comfortable but also comfortable.
It deserves five-star praise and is highly recommended. When you come to Nanxun, stay at Guanghong Ramada.
